## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) expression is:
```
2.097*epsilon**3 + 71.356*epsilon**0.2*exp(-0.6018/(T)) + 3.305*epsilon**3*(T - 370.17)
```

Simplifying: the GT has three terms:
1. `2.097*epsilon**3` — a pure epsilon**3 term
2. `71.356*epsilon**0.2*exp(-0.6018/T)` — depends on both epsilon and T via exp(-const/T)
3. `3.305*epsilon**3*(T - 370.17)` — depends on both epsilon**3 and T linearly

Combining terms 1 and 3:
`epsilon**3 * (2.097 + 3.305*T - 3.305*370.17) = epsilon**3 * (2.097 - 1223.0 + 3.305*T)`
`= epsilon**3 * (3.305*T - 1220.9) + 71.356*epsilon**0.2*exp(-0.6018/T)`

So the GT fundamentally requires:
- A term proportional to `T * epsilon**3`
- A term proportional to `epsilon**3`
- A term proportional to `epsilon**0.2 * exp(-const/T)`

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce these functional forms:

**Key requirements:**
1. Need `T * epsilon**3` (or `T * epsilon**n` for some power n=3)
2. Need `epsilon**0.2 * exp(c/T)` (exponential in 1/T times fractional power of epsilon)

Most candidates don't have T dependence at all (candidates 2-4, 7-9, 11-29, etc.) — these cannot match since the GT depends on T.

**Candidates with T dependence:**
- **1**: Has `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2` — can produce T*epsilon**3 but lacks exp(-c/T) term
- **5, 6**: Have `c9/T**5` — wrong T dependence
- **10**: Has `log(T*c7 + ...)` — wrong T dependence
- **24, 25**: Have `exp(T*c6)` — wrong T dependence (exp(T) vs exp(1/T))
- **30**: `T*c0 + ...` — linear in T but no T*epsilon**3 coupling, and no exp(-c/T)
- **31**: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**2` — has T*epsilon**2, not T*epsilon**3, and no exp(-c/T)
- **32**: `T*c0 + ...` — no T*epsilon coupling
- **34**: Has `exp(c4/T)` and `sin` terms — has exp(c/T) but needs epsilon**0.2 multiplied by it. The exp(c4/T) term is `c3*exp(c4/T)` with no epsilon dependence. Cannot produce `epsilon**0.2 * exp(-c/T)`.
- **38**: Has `exp(c4/T)` — same issue, exp(c4/T) not multiplied by epsilon**0.2
- **39**: `T*c0 + ... + c8*exp(c9/T)` — has T*c0 (linear T, no epsilon coupling needed for T*epsilon**3) and exp(c/T) without epsilon**0.2 factor. Cannot match.
- **42**: Has `/T**5` — wrong T dependence
- **47**: Has `1/T**5` — wrong
- **48**: Has `cos(T*c3)` — wrong T dependence

**Candidate 1** is closest with `T*c1*epsilon**c2` for the T*epsilon**3 term, but it lacks `exp(-c/T)` which is essential.

**Candidate 39** has both `T*c0` and `exp(c9/T)`, but `T*c0` is just linear in T (no epsilon**3 coupling), and `exp(c9/T)` has no epsilon**0.2 factor. The epsilon terms don't couple correctly with T.

No candidate can simultaneously produce:
- `T * epsilon**3`
- `epsilon**0.2 * exp(-const/T)`

Conclusion: No match
